document.addEventListener('click', closeVideo);

function closeVideo() {
    if(document.querySelector('.dialog-lightbox-message')){
        const videoContainer = document.querySelector('.dialog-lightbox-message');
        
        videoContainer.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if(e.target !== document.querySelector('video')){
                document.querySelector('.dialog-lightbox-widget').style.display = 'none';
                if(videoContainer.firstChild){
                    videoContainer.removeChild(videoContainer.firstChild);
                }
            }
            
        })
    }
}
</script>		</div>
